var kills = 10;

setInterval(getkills, 250);

function getkills(){
    var count = parseInt(document.getElementById("killCounter").innerText);
    if(count > kills){
        setTimeout(() => {
            doNewSend(["ch", ["Bawlan kill: "+count]]);
        },0);
        setTimeout(() => {
            doNewSend(["ch", ["Bawlan Is The Best"]]);
        },1500);
        setTimeout(() => {
           doNewSend(["ch", ["Bawlan have Op insta"]]);
        },3000);
    }
    kills = count;
}
function doNewSend(sender){
    ws.send(new Uint8Array(Array.from(msgpack5.encode(sender))));
}
